OBJECT Report 11012902 Project Cash Flow
{
  OBJECT-PROPERTIES
  {
    Date=;
    Time=;
    Version List=4PS14.00;
  }
  PROPERTIES
  {
    CaptionML=[DEU=Projekt Cash-flow;
               ENU=Project Cash Flow;
               NLD=Projectkasstroom;
               SVE=Projektets kassaflîde];
    OnInitReport=BEGIN
                   IF (ReferenceDate = 0D) THEN BEGIN
                     PeriodType := PeriodType::Year;
                     ReferenceDate := TODAY;
                     RoundFactor := RoundFactor::"1";
                   END;
                 END;

    OnPreReport=VAR
                  lvDateRec@1100525001 : Record 2000000007;
                  lvExtraActualPeriod@1100525000 : Boolean;
                BEGIN
                  IF (ReferenceDate = 0D) THEN
                    ERROR(Text000);

                  CASE RoundFactor OF
                    RoundFactor::"1000":
                      RoundTxt := Text001;
                    RoundFactor::"1000000":
                      RoundTxt := Text002;
                    ELSE
                      RoundTxt := '';
                  END;

                  CASE ReportType OF
                    ReportType::"Actual and Budget":
                      BEGIN
                        NoOfColumn := 8;
                        LastActualColumn := 4;
                      END;
                    ReportType::"Actual and Budget with extra Years":
                      BEGIN
                        NoOfColumn := 10;
                        LastActualColumn := 5;
                      END;
                    ReportType::"Extra Years":
                      BEGIN
                        NoOfColumn := 12;
                        LastActualColumn := 6;
                      END;
                  END;

                  lvDateRec."Period Start" := ReferenceDate;
                  PeriodFormManagementCU.FindDate('', lvDateRec, PeriodType);
                  IF (lvDateRec."Period Start" = ReferenceDate) AND (LastActualColumn >= 1) THEN
                    lvExtraActualPeriod := TRUE;  //* Last Actual Period is equal to First Budget Period not needed
                  IF (LastActualColumn > 1) THEN
                    PeriodFormManagementCU.NextDate((1 - LastActualColumn), lvDateRec, PeriodType);
                  IF (lvExtraActualPeriod) THEN
                    PeriodFormManagementCU.NextDate(-1, lvDateRec, PeriodType);
                  FOR Counter := 1 TO NoOfColumn DO BEGIN
                    StartDateArray[Counter] := lvDateRec."Period Start";
                    EndDateArray[Counter] := lvDateRec."Period End";
                    HeaderArray[Counter] := PeriodFormManagementCU.CreatePeriodFormat(PeriodType, lvDateRec."Period Start");
                    IF (Counter <> LastActualColumn) OR (lvExtraActualPeriod) THEN
                      //* Last Actual Period is equal to First Budget Period (two columns with same period)
                      PeriodFormManagementCU.NextDate(1, lvDateRec, PeriodType);
                  END;

                  AmntFormatExpr := ProjDevelopmentCU.GetAmntFormatExprForPrinting(RoundFactor);
                END;

  }
  DATASET

    { 1100525006;1;DataItem;                 ;
               DataItemTable=Table11012913;
               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  //* Note: Order of execution is important!
                                  RubricActual := CalculateRubricActual();
                                  RubricBudget := CalculateRubricBudget();
                                  RubricTotal := CalculateRubricTotal();
                                  CalculatePeriodAmounts();

                                  PercentActTxt := '';  //*15625.n
                                  PercentBudTxt := '';  //*15625.n
                                  PercentTxt := '';
                                  AmntFormatExpr2 := AmntFormatExpr;
                                  CASE Type OF
                                    Type::Costs,
                                    Type::Revenues,
                                    Type::"Percentage Costs",
                                    Type::"Percentage Revenues",
                                    Type::"Costs as Perc. Revenues",
                                    Type::"Revenues as Perc. Costs",
                                    Type::"Costs to Distr. as Perc. Rev.",
                                    Type::Subtotal,
                                    Type::Balance,
                                    Type::EPV:
                                      BEGIN
                                        ProjDevelopmentCU.RoundAmountForPrinting(RubricActual, RoundFactor);
                                        ProjDevelopmentCU.RoundAmountForPrinting(RubricBudget, RoundFactor);
                                        ProjDevelopmentCU.RoundAmountForPrinting(RubricTotal, RoundFactor);
                                        FOR Counter := 1 TO NoOfColumn DO BEGIN
                                          ProjDevelopmentCU.RoundAmountForPrinting(AmntArray[Counter], RoundFactor);
                                        END;
                                      END;
                                    Type::"Perc. (Sub)Totals":  //*15625.n
                                      BEGIN
                                        IF (RubricActual <> 0) THEN
                                          PercentActTxt := '%';
                                        IF (RubricBudget <> 0) THEN
                                          PercentBudTxt := '%';
                                        IF (RubricTotal <> 0) THEN
                                          PercentTxt := '%';
                                        AmntFormatExpr2 := '#,##0.00';
                                      END;
                                    Type::ROS,
                                    Type::PRI:
                                      IF (RubricTotal <> 0) THEN BEGIN
                                        PercentTxt := '%';
                                        AmntFormatExpr2 := '#,##0.00';
                                      END;
                                  END;

                                  RubricCode := "Rubric Code";
                                  IF (Type = Type::Line) OR ((Type = Type::Text) AND (Description = '')) THEN
                                    RubricCode := ''
                                END;

               ReqFilterFields=Rubric Code;
               DataItemLink=Project No.=FIELD(Project No.),
                            Version=FIELD(Version) }

    { 1100525034;2;Column;Type_InvestmProposalRubricLine;
               SourceExpr=FORMAT(Type,0,2) }

  CODE
  {
    VAR
      ProjDevelopmentCU@1100525025 : Codeunit 11012903;
      PeriodFormManagementCU@1100525024 : Codeunit 359;
      PeriodType@1100525023 : 'Day,Week,Month,Quarter,Year';
      RoundFactor@1100525022 : 'None,1,1000,1000000';
      SplitType@1100525021 : 'Actual,Budget,Both';
      ReferenceDate@1100525020 : Date;
      Date_StartPeriod@1100525019 : Date;
      Date_EndPeriod@1100525018 : Date;
      StartDateArray@1100525017 : ARRAY [12] OF Date;
      EndDateArray@1100525016 : ARRAY [12] OF Date;
      ReportType@1100525014 : 'Actual and Budget,Actual and Budget with extra Years,Extra Years';
      Counter@1100525013 : Integer;
      NoOfColumn@1100525012 : Integer;
      LastActualColumn@1100525011 : Integer;
      RubricActual@1100525010 : Decimal;
      RubricBudget@1100525009 : Decimal;
      RubricTotal@1100525008 : Decimal;
      AmntArray@1100525007 : ARRAY [12] OF Decimal;
      RubricCode@1100525006 : Code[10];
      RoundTxt@1100525005 : Text[30];
      PercentTxt@1100525003 : Text[10];
      PercentActTxt@1100525002 : Text[10];
      PercentBudTxt@1100525001 : Text[10];
      HeaderArray@1100525000 : ARRAY [12] OF Text[30];
      Text000@1100525028 : TextConst 'DEU=Referenzdatum ist nicht eingegeben worden.;ENU=Reference Date is not filled.;NLD=Referentiedatum is niet gevuld.';
      Text001@1100525027 : TextConst 'DEU=BetrÑge x 1000;ENU=Amounts x 1000;NLD=Bedragen x 1000';
      Text002@1100525026 : TextConst 'DEU=BetrÑge x Million;ENU=Amounts x million;NLD=Bedragen x miljioen';
      AmntFormatExpr@1100525033 : Text[30];
      AmntFormatExpr2@1100528700 : Text[30];

    PROCEDURE GetReportName@1100525003() : Text;
    BEGIN
      EXIT(DELSTR(CurrReport.OBJECTID, 1, STRPOS(CurrReport.OBJECTID, ' ')));
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetReportFilter@1100525000() : Text;
    BEGIN
      IF "Investm. Proposal Rubric Line".GETFILTERS <> '' THEN
        EXIT(STRSUBSTNO('%1: %2', "Investm. Proposal Rubric Line".TABLECAPTION, "Investm. Proposal Rubric Line".GETFILTERS));
    END;

    PROCEDURE CalculateRubricActual@1210190007() : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      WITH "Investm. Proposal Rubric Line" DO BEGIN
        CASE Type OF
          Type::Costs,
          Type::Revenues,
          Type::"Percentage Costs",
          Type::"Percentage Revenues",
          Type::"Costs as Perc. Revenues",
          Type::"Revenues as Perc. Costs",
          Type::"Costs to Distr. as Perc. Rev.",
          Type::"Perc. (Sub)Totals",  //*15625.n
          Type::Subtotal,
          Type::Balance:
            EXIT(ProjDevelopmentCU.CalculateActualByRubric("Investm. Proposal Rubric Line", 0D, 0D, ReferenceDate));
        END;
        EXIT(0);
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE CalculateRubricBudget@1210190011() : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      WITH "Investm. Proposal Rubric Line" DO BEGIN
        CASE Type OF
          Type::Costs,
          Type::Revenues,
          Type::"Percentage Costs",
          Type::"Percentage Revenues",
          Type::"Costs as Perc. Revenues",
          Type::"Revenues as Perc. Costs",
          Type::"Costs to Distr. as Perc. Rev.",
          Type::"Perc. (Sub)Totals",  //*15625.n
          Type::Subtotal,
          Type::Balance:
            EXIT(ProjDevelopmentCU.CalculateBudgetByRubric("Investm. Proposal Rubric Line", 0D, 0D, ReferenceDate));
        END;
        EXIT(0);
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE CalculateRubricTotal@1210190010() : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      WITH "Investm. Proposal Rubric Line" DO BEGIN
        CASE Type OF
          Type::Costs,
          Type::Revenues,
          Type::"Percentage Costs",
          Type::"Percentage Revenues",
          Type::"Costs as Perc. Revenues",
          Type::"Revenues as Perc. Costs",
          Type::"Costs to Distr. as Perc. Rev.",
          Type::Subtotal,
          Type::Balance:
            EXIT(RubricActual + RubricBudget);
          Type::"Perc. (Sub)Totals":  //*15625.n
            EXIT(ProjDevelopmentCU.CalculatePercRubricsTotActBudg("Investm. Proposal Rubric Line", 0D, 0D, ReferenceDate));
          Type::ROS:
            EXIT(ProjDevelopmentCU.CalculateTotalRos("Project No.", Version, ReferenceDate, FALSE));
          Type::EPV:
            EXIT(ProjDevelopmentCU.CalculateTotalEPV("Project No.", Version, ReferenceDate, PeriodType, FALSE));
          Type::PRI:
            EXIT(ProjDevelopmentCU.CalculateTotalPRI("Project No.", Version, ReferenceDate, PeriodType, FALSE));
        END;
        EXIT(0);
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE CalculatePeriodAmounts@1210190006();
    BEGIN
      WITH "Investm. Proposal Rubric Line" DO BEGIN
        CLEAR(AmntArray);
        FOR Counter := 1 TO NoOfColumn DO BEGIN
          CASE Type OF
            Type::Costs,
            Type::Revenues,
            Type::"Percentage Costs",
            Type::"Percentage Revenues",
            Type::"Costs as Perc. Revenues",
            Type::"Revenues as Perc. Costs",
            Type::"Costs to Distr. as Perc. Rev.",
            Type::Subtotal,
            Type::Balance:
              BEGIN
                IF Counter <= LastActualColumn THEN
                  AmntArray[Counter] := ProjDevelopmentCU.CalculateActualByRubric("Investm. Proposal Rubric Line",
                                              GetStartDate(Counter), EndDateArray[Counter], ReferenceDate)
                ELSE
                  AmntArray[Counter] := ProjDevelopmentCU.CalculateBudgetByRubric("Investm. Proposal Rubric Line",
                                              StartDateArray[Counter], GetEndDate(Counter), ReferenceDate);
              END;
            Type::EPV:
              BEGIN
                Date_StartPeriod := StartDateArray[Counter];
                Date_EndPeriod := EndDateArray[Counter];
                IF Counter <= LastActualColumn THEN BEGIN
                  IF Counter = 1 THEN
                    Date_StartPeriod := 0D;  //* Hierdoor EPV t/m eerste periode (kolom 'Period..')
                  SplitType := SplitType::Actual;
                END ELSE BEGIN
                  IF Counter = NoOfColumn THEN
                    Date_EndPeriod := 0D;  //* Hierdoor EPV vanaf laatste periode (kolom 'Period..')
                  SplitType := SplitType::Budget;
                END;
                AmntArray[Counter] :=
                  ProjDevelopmentCU.CalculatePeriodEPV(
                    "Project No.", Version, ReferenceDate, PeriodType,
                    Date_StartPeriod, Date_EndPeriod, SplitType, FALSE);
              END;
          END;
        END;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetStartDate@1210190002(ICounter@1210190001 : Integer) : Date;
    BEGIN
      IF ICounter > 1 THEN
        EXIT(StartDateArray[ICounter])
      ELSE
      //  EXIT(DMY2DATE(1, 1, 1));  //* Not 0D !
        EXIT(0D);
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetEndDate@1210190001(ICounter@1210190001 : Integer) : Date;
    BEGIN
      IF ICounter < NoOfColumn THEN
        EXIT(EndDateArray[ICounter])
      ELSE
        EXIT(NORMALDATE(EndDateArray[ICounter]) + 36500);
    END;

    BEGIN
    END.
  }

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value = 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Shared offset As Integer
Shared newgroup As Object
Shared currentgroup1 As Object
Shared currentgroup2 As Object

Public Function GetGroupPageNumber(newgroup2 As Boolean, pagenumber As Integer) As Object
    If newgroup2
        offset = pagenumber - 1
    End If
    Return pagenumber - offset
End Function

Public Function InNewGroup(group1 As Object, group2 As Object) As Boolean
    newgroup = False
    If Not (group1 = currentgroup1)
        newgroup = True
        currentgroup2 = group2
        currentgroup1 = group1
    Else
        If Not (group2 = currentgroup2)
            newgroup = True
            currentgroup2 = group2
        End If
    End If
    Return newgroup
End Function

Shared Data1 As Object

Public Function GetData(Num As Integer) As Object
    Return Cstr(Choose(Num, Split(Cstr(Data1), Chr(177))))
End Function

Public Function SetData(NewData As Object)
    If NewData &lt;&gt; "" Then
        Data1 = NewData
    End If
End Function
